```typescript
49	export function logo(pad?: string) {
50	  if (!process.stdout.isTTY && !process.stderr.isTTY) {
51	    const result = []
52	    for (const row of wordmark) {
53	      if (pad) result.push(pad)
54	      result.push(row)
55	      result.push(EOL)
56	    }
57	    return result.join("").trimEnd()
58	  }
59	
60	  const result: string[] = []
61	  const reset = "\x1b[0m"
62	  const left = {
63	    fg: "\x1b[90m",
64	    shadow: "\x1b[38;5;235m",
65	    bg: "\x1b[48;5;235m",
66	  }
67	  const right = {
68	    fg: reset,
69	    shadow: "\x1b[38;5;238m",
70	    bg: "\x1b[48;5;238m",
71	  }
72	  const gap = "  "
73	  const draw = (line: string, fg: string, shadow: string, bg: string) => {
74	    const parts: string[] = []
75	    for (const char of line) {
76	      if (char === "_") {
77	        parts.push(bg, " ", reset)
78	        continue
79	      }
80	      if (char === "^") {
81	        parts.push(fg, bg, "▀", reset)
82	        continue
83	      }
84	      if (char === "~") {
85	        parts.push(shadow, "▀", reset)
86	        continue
87	      }
88	      if (char === " ") {
89	        parts.push(" ")
90	        continue
91	      }
92	      parts.push(fg, char, reset)
93	    }
94	    return parts.join("")
95	  }
96	  glyphs.left.forEach((row, index) => {
97	    if (pad) result.push(pad)
98	    result.push(draw(row, left.fg, left.shadow, left.bg))
99	    result.push(gap)
100	    const other = glyphs.right[index] ?? ""
101	    result.push(draw(other, right.fg, right.shadow, right.bg))
102	    result.push(EOL)
103	  })
104	  return result.join("").trimEnd()
105	}

107	export async function input(prompt: string): Promise<string> {
108	  const readline = require("readline")
109	  const rl = readline.createInterface({
110	    input: process.stdin,
111	    output: process.stdout,
112	  })
113	
114	  return new Promise((resolve) => {
115	    rl.question(prompt, (answer: string) => {
116	      rl.close()
117	      resolve(answer.trim())
118	    })
119	  })
120	}
```

#### packages/opencode/src/tool/bash-interactive.ts — request(function)

```typescript
1	import { Deferred, Effect, Layer, Context } from "effect"
2	import { Bus } from "@/bus"
3	import { BusEvent } from "@/bus/bus-event"
4	import { InstanceState } from "@/effect"
5	import { Log } from "@/util"
6	import z from "zod"
7	import crypto from "crypto"
8	
9	const log = Log.create({ service: "bash-interactive" })
10	
11	// Bus events
12	
13	export const Event = {
14	  Asked: BusEvent.define(
15	    "bash.interactive.asked",
16	    z.object({
17	      id: z.string(),
18	      command: z.string(),
19	      cwd: z.string(),
20	      env: z.record(z.string(), z.string()).optional(),
21	      description: z.string(),
22	    }),
23	  ),
24	  Replied: BusEvent.define(
25	    "bash.interactive.replied",
26	    z.object({
27	      id: z.string(),
28	      output: z.string(),
29	      exitCode: z.number(),
30	    }),
31	  ),
32	}
33	
34	// Types
35	
36	export interface InteractiveRequest {
37	  id: string
38	  command: string
39	  cwd: string
40	  env?: Record<string, string>
41	  description: string
42	}
43	
44	export interface InteractiveResult {
45	  output: string
46	  exitCode: number
47	}
48	
49	export class InteractiveError extends Error {
50	  constructor(message: string) {
51	    super(message)
52	    this.name = "BashInteractiveError"
53	  }
54	}
55	
56	// Service
57	
58	interface PendingEntry {
59	  request: InteractiveRequest
60	  deferred: Deferred.Deferred<InteractiveResult, InteractiveError>
61	}
62	
63	interface State {
64	  pending: Map<string, PendingEntry>
65	}
66	
67	export interface Interface {
68	  readonly request: (input: {
69	    command: string
70	    cwd: string
71	    env?: Record<string, string>
72	    description: string
73	  }) => Effect.Effect<InteractiveResult, InteractiveError>
74	  readonly reply: (input: { id: string; output: string; exitCode: number }) => Effect.Effect<void>
75	  readonly list: () => Effect.Effect<ReadonlyArray<InteractiveRequest>>
76	}
77	
78	export class Service extends Context.Service<Service, Interface>()("@opencode/BashInteractive") {}
79	
80	export const layer = Layer.effect(
81	  Service,
82	  Effect.gen(function* () {
83	    const bus = yield* Bus.Service
84	    const state = yield* InstanceState.make<State>(
85	      Effect.fn("BashInteractive.state")(function* () {
86	        const state: State = {
87	          pending: new Map(),
88	        }
89	
90	        yield* Effect.addFinalizer(() =>
91	          Effect.gen(function* () {
92	            for (const item of state.pending.values()) {
93	              yield* Deferred.fail(item.deferred, new InteractiveError("Instance disposed"))
94	            }
95	            state.pending.clear()
96	          }),
97	        )
98	
99	        return state
100	      }),
101	    )
102	
103	    const request = Effect.fn("BashInteractive.request")(function* (input: {
104	      command: string
105	      cwd: string
106	      env?: Record<string, string>
107	      description: string
108	    }) {
109	      const pending = (yield* InstanceState.get(state)).pending
110	      const id = crypto.randomUUID()
111	      log.info("requesting interactive", { id, command: input.command })
112	
113	      const deferred = yield* Deferred.make<InteractiveResult, InteractiveError>()
114	      const req: InteractiveRequest = {
115	        id,
116	        command: input.command,
117	        cwd: input.cwd,
118	        env: input.env,
119	        description: input.description,
120	      }
121	      pending.set(id, { request: req, deferred })
122	      yield* bus.publish(Event.Asked, req)
123	
124	      return yield* Effect.ensuring(
125	        Deferred.await(deferred),
126	        Effect.sync(() => {
127	          pending.delete(id)
128	        }),
129	      )
130	    })
131	
132	    const reply = Effect.fn("BashInteractive.reply")(function* (input: {
133	      id: string
134	      output: string
135	      exitCode: number
136	    }) {
137	      const pending = (yield* InstanceState.get(state)).pending
138	      const existing = pending.get(input.id)
139	      if (!existing) {
140	        log.warn("reply for unknown request", { id: input.id })
141	        return
142	      }
143	      pending.delete(input.id)
144	      log.info("replied", { id: input.id, exitCode: input.exitCode })
145	      yield* bus.publish(Event.Replied, {
146	        id: existing.request.id,
147	        output: input.output,
148	        exitCode: input.exitCode,
149	      })
150	      yield* Deferred.succeed(existing.deferred, {
151	        output: input.output,
152	        exitCode: input.exitCode,
153	      })
154	    })
155	
156	    const list = Effect.fn("BashInteractive.list")(function* () {
157	      const pending = (yield* InstanceState.get(state)).pending
158	      return Array.from(pending.values(), (x) => x.request)
159	    })
160	
161	    return Service.of({ request, reply, list })
162	  }),
163	)
164	
165	export const defaultLayer = layer.pipe(Layer.provide(Bus.layer))
166	
167	// Standalone functions (uses the instance-scoped runtime, same pattern as Bus module)
168	import { makeRuntime } from "@/effect/run-service"
169	
170	const { runPromise } = makeRuntime(Service, defaultLayer)
171	
172	export function request(input: {
173	  command: string
174	  cwd: string
175	  env?: Record<string, string>
176	  description: string
177	}): Promise<InteractiveResult> {
178	  return runPromise((svc) => svc.request(input))
179	}
180	
181	export function reply(input: { id: string; output: string; exitCode: number }): Promise<void> {
182	  return runPromise((svc) => svc.reply(input))
183	}
```

#### packages/opencode/src/provider/error.ts — message(function)

```typescript
1	import { APICallError } from "ai"
2	import { STATUS_CODES } from "http"
3	import { iife } from "@/util/iife"
4	import type { ProviderID } from "./schema"
5	
6	// Adapted from overflow detection patterns in:
7	// https://github.com/badlogic/pi-mono/blob/main/packages/ai/src/utils/overflow.ts
8	const OVERFLOW_PATTERNS = [
9	  /prompt is too long/i, // Anthropic
10	  /input is too long for requested model/i, // Amazon Bedrock
11	  /exceeds the context window/i, // OpenAI (Completions + Responses API message text)
12	  /input token count.*exceeds the maximum/i, // Google (Gemini)
13	  /maximum prompt length is \d+/i, // xAI (Grok)
14	  /reduce the length of the messages/i, // Groq
15	  /maximum context length is \d+ tokens/i, // OpenRouter, DeepSeek, vLLM
16	  /exceeds the limit of \d+/i, // GitHub Copilot
17	  /exceeds the available context size/i, // llama.cpp server
18	  /greater than the context length/i, // LM Studio
19	  /context window exceeds limit/i, // MiniMax
20	  /exceeded model token limit/i, // Kimi For Coding, Moonshot
21	  /context[_ ]length[_ ]exceeded/i, // Generic fallback
22	  /request entity too large/i, // HTTP 413
23	  /context length is only \d+ tokens/i, // vLLM
24	  /input length.*exceeds.*context length/i, // vLLM
25	  /prompt too long; exceeded (?:max )?context length/i, // Ollama explicit overflow error
26	  /too large for model with \d+ maximum context length/i, // Mistral
27	  /model_context_window_exceeded/i, // z.ai non-standard finish_reason surfaced as error text
28	]
29	
30	function isOpenAiErrorRetryable(e: APICallError) {
31	  const status = e.statusCode
32	  if (!status) return e.isRetryable
33	  // openai sometimes returns 404 for models that are actually available
34	  return status === 404 || e.isRetryable
35	}
36	
37	// Providers not reliably handled in this function:
38	// - z.ai: can accept overflow silently (needs token-count/context-window checks)
39	function isOverflow(message: string) {
40	  if (OVERFLOW_PATTERNS.some((p) => p.test(message))) return true
41	
42	  // Providers/status patterns handled outside of regex list:
43	  // - Cerebras: often returns "400 (no body)" / "413 (no body)"
44	  // - Mistral: often returns "400 (no body)" / "413 (no body)"
45	  return /^4(00|13)\s*(status code)?\s*\(no body\)/i.test(message)
46	}
47	
48	// Provider IDs served by the MiMo model gateway. Its error bodies carry
49	// non-standard semantics (e.g. moderation/risk-control blocks under HTTP 400),
50	// so the gateway-specific handling below is scoped to these providers and leaves
51	// every other provider's error flow untouched.
52	const MIMO_GATEWAY_PROVIDERS = new Set(["xiaomi", "mimo"])
53	
54	// MiMo gateway error.code values worth relabeling: moderation (421) and
55	// risk-control (441) blocks arrive under a generic HTTP 400.
56	const FRIENDLY_GATEWAY_CODES: Record<string, string> = {
57	  "421": "Request blocked by content moderation",
58	  "441": "Request blocked by risk control",
59	}
60	
61	function message(providerID: ProviderID, e: APICallError) {
62	  return iife(() => {
63	    // MiMo gateway: relabel known block codes and surface error.param (the real
64	    // reason often lives there while error.message stays generic). json() returns
65	    // undefined for non-JSON, so HTML/proxy error pages fall through to the
66	    // original handling below.
67	    const gw = MIMO_GATEWAY_PROVIDERS.has(providerID) ? json(e.responseBody)?.error : undefined
68	    if (gw && typeof gw === "object") {
69	      const base = FRIENDLY_GATEWAY_CODES[String(gw.code)] ?? (typeof gw.message === "string" ? gw.message : "")
70	      if (base) return typeof gw.param === "string" && gw.param !== base ? `${base}: ${gw.param}` : base
71	    }
72	
73	    const msg = e.message
74	    if (msg === "") {
75	      if (e.responseBody) return e.responseBody
76	      if (e.statusCode) {
77	        const err = STATUS_CODES[e.statusCode]
78	        if (err) return err
79	      }
80	      return "Unknown error"
81	    }
82	
83	    if (!e.responseBody || (e.statusCode && msg !== STATUS_CODES[e.statusCode])) {
84	      return msg
85	    }
86	
87	    try {
88	      const body = JSON.parse(e.responseBody)
89	      // try to extract common error message fields
90	      const errMsg = body.message || body.error || body.error?.message
91	      if (errMsg && typeof errMsg === "string") {
92	        return `${msg}: ${errMsg}`
93	      }
94	    } catch {}
95	
96	    // If responseBody is HTML (e.g. from a gateway or proxy error page),
97	    // provide a human-readable message instead of dumping raw markup
98	    if (/^\s*<!doctype|^\s*<html/i.test(e.responseBody)) {
99	      if (e.statusCode === 401) {
100	        return "Unauthorized: request was blocked by a gateway or proxy. Your authentication token may be missing or expired — try running `opencode auth login <your provider URL>` to re-authenticate."
101	      }
102	      if (e.statusCode === 403) {
103	        return "Forbidden: request was blocked by a gateway or proxy. You may not have permission to access this resource — check your account and provider settings."
104	      }
105	      return msg
106	    }
107	
108	    return `${msg}: ${e.responseBody}`
109	  }).trim()
110	}
111	
112	function json(input: unknown) {
113	  if (typeof input === "string") {
114	    try {
115	      const result = JSON.parse(input)
116	      if (result && typeof result === "object") return result
117	      return undefined
118	    } catch {
119	      return undefined
120	    }
121	  }
122	  if (typeof input === "object" && input !== null) {
123	    return input
124	  }
125	  return undefined
126	}
127	
128	export type ParsedStreamError =
129	  | {
130	      type: "context_overflow"
131	      message: string
132	      responseBody: string
133	    }
134	  | {
135	      type: "api_error"
136	      message: string
137	      isRetryable: false
138	      responseBody: string
139	    }
140	
141	export function parseStreamError(input: unknown): ParsedStreamError | undefined {
142	  const body = json(input)
143	  if (!body) return
144	
145	  const responseBody = JSON.stringify(body)
146	  if (body.type !== "error") return
147	
148	  switch (body?.error?.code) {
149	    case "context_length_exceeded":
150	      return {
151	        type: "context_overflow",
152	        message: "Input exceeds context window of this model",
153	        responseBody,
154	      }
155	    case "insufficient_quota":
156	      return {
157	        type: "api_error",
158	        message: "Quota exceeded. Check your plan and billing details.",
159	        isRetryable: false,
160	        responseBody,
161	      }
162	    case "usage_not_included":
163	      return {
164	        type: "api_error",
165	        message: "To use Codex with your ChatGPT plan, upgrade to Plus: https://chatgpt.com/explore/plus.",
166	        isRetryable: false,
167	        responseBody,
168	      }
169	    case "invalid_prompt":
170	      return {
171	        type: "api_error",
172	        message: typeof body?.error?.message === "string" ? body?.error?.message : "Invalid prompt.",
173	        isRetryable: false,
174	        responseBody,
175	      }
176	  }
177	}
178	
179	export type ParsedAPICallError =
180	  | {
181	      type: "context_overflow"
182	      message: string
183	      responseBody?: string
184	    }
185	  | {
186	      type: "api_error"
187	      message: string
188	      statusCode?: number
189	      isRetryable: boolean
190	      responseHeaders?: Record<string, string>
191	      responseBody?: string
192	      metadata?: Record<string, string>
193	    }
194	
195	export function parseAPICallError(input: { providerID: ProviderID; error: APICallError }): ParsedAPICallError {
196	  const m = message(input.providerID, input.error)
197	  const body = json(input.error.responseBody)
198	  if (isOverflow(m) || input.error.statusCode === 413 || body?.error?.code === "context_length_exceeded") {
199	    return {
200	      type: "context_overflow",
201	      message: m,
202	      responseBody: input.error.responseBody,
203	    }
204	  }
205	
206	  const metadata = input.error.url ? { url: input.error.url } : undefined
207	  return {
208	    type: "api_error",
209	    message: m,
210	    statusCode: input.error.statusCode,
211	    isRetryable: input.providerID.startsWith("openai") ? isOpenAiErrorRetryable(input.error) : input.error.isRetryable,
212	    responseHeaders: input.error.responseHeaders,
213	    responseBody: input.error.responseBody,
214	    metadata,
215	  }
216	}
```

```typescript
49	export function logo(pad?: string) {
50	  if (!process.stdout.isTTY && !process.stderr.isTTY) {
51	    const result = []
52	    for (const row of wordmark) {
53	      if (pad) result.push(pad)
54	      result.push(row)
55	      result.push(EOL)
56	    }
57	    return result.join("").trimEnd()
58	  }
59	
60	  const result: string[] = []
61	  const reset = "\x1b[0m"
62	  const left = {
63	    fg: "\x1b[90m",
64	    shadow: "\x1b[38;5;235m",
65	    bg: "\x1b[48;5;235m",
66	  }
67	  const right = {
68	    fg: reset,
69	    shadow: "\x1b[38;5;238m",
70	    bg: "\x1b[48;5;238m",
71	  }
72	  const gap = "  "
73	  const draw = (line: string, fg: string, shadow: string, bg: string) => {
74	    const parts: string[] = []
75	    for (const char of line) {
76	      if (char === "_") {
77	        parts.push(bg, " ", reset)
78	        continue
79	      }
80	      if (char === "^") {
81	        parts.push(fg, bg, "▀", reset)
82	        continue
83	      }
84	      if (char === "~") {
85	        parts.push(shadow, "▀", reset)
86	        continue
87	      }
88	      if (char === " ") {
89	        parts.push(" ")
90	        continue
91	      }
92	      parts.push(fg, char, reset)
93	    }
94	    return parts.join("")
95	  }
96	  glyphs.left.forEach((row, index) => {
97	    if (pad) result.push(pad)
98	    result.push(draw(row, left.fg, left.shadow, left.bg))
99	    result.push(gap)
100	    const other = glyphs.right[index] ?? ""
101	    result.push(draw(other, right.fg, right.shadow, right.bg))
102	    result.push(EOL)
103	  })
104	  return result.join("").trimEnd()
105	}

107	export async function input(prompt: string): Promise<string> {
108	  const readline = require("readline")
109	  const rl = readline.createInterface({
110	    input: process.stdin,
111	    output: process.stdout,
112	  })
113	
114	  return new Promise((resolve) => {
115	    rl.question(prompt, (answer: string) => {
116	      rl.close()
117	      resolve(answer.trim())
118	    })
119	  })
120	}

125	  }
126	  println(Style.TEXT_DANGER_BOLD + "Error: " + Style.TEXT_NORMAL + message)
127	}
```

```typescript
1300	  async prompt(params: PromptRequest) {
1301	    const sessionID = params.sessionId
1302	    const session = this.sessionManager.get(sessionID)
1303	    const directory = session.cwd
1304	
1305	    const current = session.model
1306	    const model = current ?? (await defaultModel(this.config, directory))
1307	    if (!current) {
1308	      this.sessionManager.setModel(session.id, model)
1309	    }
1310	    const agent = session.modeId ?? (await AppRuntime.runPromise(AgentModule.Service.use((svc) => svc.defaultAgent())))
1311	
1312	    const parts: Array<
1313	      | { type: "text"; text: string; synthetic?: boolean; ignored?: boolean }
1314	      | { type: "file"; url: string; filename: string; mime: string }
1315	    > = []
1316	    for (const part of params.prompt) {
1317	      switch (part.type) {
1318	        case "text":
1319	          const audience = part.annotations?.audience
1320	          const forAssistant = audience?.length === 1 && audience[0] === "assistant"
1321	          const forUser = audience?.length === 1 && audience[0] === "user"
1322	          parts.push({
1323	            type: "text" as const,
1324	            text: part.text,
1325	            ...(forAssistant && { synthetic: true }),
1326	            ...(forUser && { ignored: true }),
1327	          })
1328	          break
1329	        case "image": {
1330	          const parsed = parseUri(part.uri ?? "")
1331	          const filename = parsed.type === "file" ? parsed.filename : "image"
1332	          if (part.data) {
1333	            parts.push({
1334	              type: "file",
1335	              url: `data:${part.mimeType};base64,${part.data}`,
1336	              filename,
1337	              mime: part.mimeType,
1338	            })
1339	          } else if (part.uri && part.uri.startsWith("http:")) {
1340	            parts.push({
1341	              type: "file",
1342	              url: part.uri,
1343	              filename,
1344	              mime: part.mimeType,
1345	            })
1346	          }
1347	          break
1348	        }
1349	
1350	        case "resource_link":
1351	          const parsed = parseUri(part.uri)
1352	          // Use the name from resource_link if available
1353	          if (part.name && parsed.type === "file") {
1354	            parsed.filename = part.name
1355	          }
1356	          parts.push(parsed)
1357	
1358	          break
1359	
1360	        case "resource": {
1361	          const resource = part.resource
1362	          if ("text" in resource && resource.text) {
1363	            parts.push({
1364	              type: "text",
1365	              text: resource.text,
1366	            })
1367	          } else if ("blob" in resource && resource.blob && resource.mimeType) {
1368	            // Binary resource (PDFs, etc.): store as file part with data URL
1369	            const parsed = parseUri(resource.uri ?? "")
1370	            const filename = parsed.type === "file" ? parsed.filename : "file"
1371	            parts.push({
1372	              type: "file",
1373	              url: `data:${resource.mimeType};base64,${resource.blob}`,
1374	              filename,
1375	              mime: resource.mimeType,
1376	            })
1377	          }
1378	          break
1379	        }
1380	
1381	        default:
1382	          break
1383	      }
1384	    }
1385	
1386	    log.info("parts", { parts })
1387	
1388	    const cmd = (() => {
1389	      const text = parts
1390	        .filter((p): p is { type: "text"; text: string } => p.type === "text")
1391	        .map((p) => p.text)
1392	        .join("")
1393	        .trim()
1394	
1395	      if (!text.startsWith("/")) return
1396	
1397	      const [name, ...rest] = text.slice(1).split(/\s+/)
1398	      return { name, args: rest.join(" ").trim() }
1399	    })()
1400	
1401	    const buildUsage = (msg: AssistantMessage): Usage => ({
1402	      totalTokens:
1403	        msg.tokens.input +
1404	        msg.tokens.output +
1405	        msg.tokens.reasoning +
1406	        (msg.tokens.cache?.read ?? 0) +
1407	        (msg.tokens.cache?.write ?? 0),
1408	      inputTokens: msg.tokens.input,
1409	      outputTokens: msg.tokens.output,
1410	      thoughtTokens: msg.tokens.reasoning || undefined,
1411	      cachedReadTokens: msg.tokens.cache?.read || undefined,
1412	      cachedWriteTokens: msg.tokens.cache?.write || undefined,
1413	    })
1414	
1415	    if (!cmd) {
1416	      const response = await this.sdk.session.prompt({
1417	        sessionID,
1418	        model: {
1419	          providerID: model.providerID,
```

```typescript
393	        UI.println(UI.Style.TEXT_INFO_BOLD + "~  " + res.data.share.url)

395	    }
```

```typescript

1300	  async prompt(params: PromptRequest) {
1301	    const sessionID = params.sessionId
1302	    const session = this.sessionManager.get(sessionID)
1303	    const directory = session.cwd
1304	
1305	    const current = session.model
1306	    const model = current ?? (await defaultModel(this.config, directory))
1307	    if (!current) {
1308	      this.sessionManager.setModel(session.id, model)
1309	    }
1310	    const agent = session.modeId ?? (await AppRuntime.runPromise(AgentModule.Service.use((svc) => svc.defaultAgent())))
1311	
1312	    const parts: Array<
1313	      | { type: "text"; text: string; synthetic?: boolean; ignored?: boolean }
1314	      | { type: "file"; url: string; filename: string; mime: string }
1315	    > = []
1316	    for (const part of params.prompt) {
1317	      switch (part.type) {
1318	        case "text":
1319	          const audience = part.annotations?.audience
1320	          const forAssistant = audience?.length === 1 && audience[0] === "assistant"
1321	          const forUser = audience?.length === 1 && audience[0] === "user"
1322	          parts.push({
1323	            type: "text" as const,
1324	            text: part.text,
1325	            ...(forAssistant && { synthetic: true }),
1326	            ...(forUser && { ignored: true }),
1327	          })
1328	          break
1329	        case "image": {
1330	          const parsed = parseUri(part.uri ?? "")
1331	          const filename = parsed.type === "file" ? parsed.filename : "image"
1332	          if (part.data) {
1333	            parts.push({
1334	              type: "file",
1335	              url: `data:${part.mimeType};base64,${part.data}`,
1336	              filename,
1337	              mime: part.mimeType,
1338	            })
1339	          } else if (part.uri && part.uri.startsWith("http:")) {
1340	            parts.push({
1341	              type: "file",
1342	              url: part.uri,
1343	              filename,
1344	              mime: part.mimeType,
1345	            })
1346	          }
1347	          break
1348	        }
1349	
1350	        case "resource_link":
1351	          const parsed = parseUri(part.uri)
1352	          // Use the name from resource_link if available
1353	          if (part.name && parsed.type === "file") {
1354	            parsed.filename = part.name
1355	          }
1356	          parts.push(parsed)
1357	
1358	          break
1359	
1360	        case "resource": {
1361	          const resource = part.resource
1362	          if ("text" in resource && resource.text) {
1363	            parts.push({
1364	              type: "text",
1365	              text: resource.text,
1366	            })
1367	          } else if ("blob" in resource && resource.blob && resource.mimeType) {
1368	            // Binary resource (PDFs, etc.): store as file part with data URL
1369	            const parsed = parseUri(resource.uri ?? "")
1370	            const filename = parsed.type === "file" ? parsed.filename : "file"
1371	            parts.push({
1372	              type: "file",
1373	              url: `data:${resource.mimeType};base64,${resource.blob}`,
1374	              filename,
1375	              mime: resource.mimeType,
1376	            })
1377	          }
1378	          break
1379	        }
1380	
1381	        default:
1382	          break
1383	      }
1384	    }
1385	
1386	    log.info("parts", { parts })
1387	
1388	    const cmd = (() => {
1389	      const text = parts
1390	        .filter((p): p is { type: "text"; text: string } => p.type === "text")
1391	        .map((p) => p.text)
1392	        .join("")
1393	        .trim()
1394	
1395	      if (!text.startsWith("/")) return
1396	
1397	      const [name, ...rest] = text.slice(1).split(/\s+/)
1398	      return { name, args: rest.join(" ").trim() }
1399	    })()
1400	
1401	    const buildUsage = (msg: AssistantMessage): Usage => ({
1402	      totalTokens:
1403	        msg.tokens.input +
1404	        msg.tokens.output +
1405	        msg.tokens.reasoning +
1406	        (msg.tokens.cache?.read ?? 0) +
1407	        (msg.tokens.cache?.write ?? 0),
1408	      inputTokens: msg.tokens.input,
1409	      outputTokens: msg.tokens.output,
1410	      thoughtTokens: msg.tokens.reasoning || undefined,
1411	      cachedReadTokens: msg.tokens.cache?.read || undefined,
1412	      cachedWriteTokens: msg.tokens.cache?.write || undefined,
1413	    })
1414	
1415	    if (!cmd) {
1416	      const response = await this.sdk.session.prompt({
1417	        sessionID,
1418	        model: {
1419	          providerID: model.providerID,
1420	          modelID: model.modelID,
1421	        },
1422	        variant: this.sessionManager.getVariant(sessionID),
1423	        parts,
1424	        agent,
1425	        directory,
1426	      })
1427	      const msg = response.data?.info
1428	
1429	      await sendUsageUpdate(this.connection, this.sdk, sessionID, directory)
1430	
1431	      return {
1432	        stopReason: "end_turn" as const,
1433	        usage: msg ? buildUsage(msg) : undefined,
1434	        _meta: {},
1435	      }
1436	    }
1437	
1438	    const command = await this.config.sdk.command
1439	      .list({ directory }, { throwOnError: true })
1440	      .then((x) => x.data!.find((c) => c.name === cmd.name))
1441	    if (command) {
1442	      const response = await this.sdk.session.command({
1443	        sessionID,
1444	        command: command.name,
1445	        arguments: cmd.args,
1446	        model: model.providerID + "/" + model.modelID,
1447	        agent,
1448	        directory,
1449	      })
1450	      const msg = response.data?.info
1451	
1452	      await sendUsageUpdate(this.connection, this.sdk, sessionID, directory)
1453	
1454	      return {
1455	        stopReason: "end_turn" as const,
1456	        usage: msg ? buildUsage(msg) : undefined,
1457	        _meta: {},
1458	      }
1459	    }
1460	
1461	    switch (cmd.name) {
1462	      case "compact":
1463	        await this.config.sdk.session.summarize(
1464	          {
1465	            sessionID,
1466	            directory,
1467	            providerID: model.providerID,
1468	            modelID: model.modelID,
1469	          },
1470	          { throwOnError: true },
1471	        )
1472	        break
1473	    }
1474	
1475	    await sendUsageUpdate(this.connection, this.sdk, sessionID, directory)
1476	
1477	    return {
1478	      stopReason: "end_turn" as const,
1479	      _meta: {},
1480	    }
1481	  }
```

#### packages/opencode/src/cli/heap.ts — start(function)

```typescript
1	import path from "path"
2	import { writeHeapSnapshot } from "node:v8"
3	import { Flag } from "@/flag/flag"
4	import { Global } from "@/global"
5	import { Log } from "@/util"
6	
7	const log = Log.create({ service: "heap" })
8	const MINUTE = 60_000
9	const LIMIT = 2 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024
10	
11	let timer: Timer | undefined
12	let lock = false
13	let armed = true
14	
15	export function start() {
16	  if (!Flag.MIMOCODE_AUTO_HEAP_SNAPSHOT) return
17	  if (timer) return
18	
19	  const run = async () => {
20	    if (lock) return
21	
22	    const stat = process.memoryUsage()
23	    if (stat.rss <= LIMIT) {
24	      armed = true
25	      return
26	    }
27	    if (!armed) return
28	
29	    lock = true
30	    armed = false
31	    const file = path.join(
32	      Global.Path.log,
33	      `heap-${process.pid}-${new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, "")}.heapsnapshot`,
34	    )
35	    log.warn("heap usage exceeded limit", {
36	      rss: stat.rss,
37	      heap: stat.heapUsed,
38	      file,
39	    })
40	
41	    await Promise.resolve()
42	      .then(() => writeHeapSnapshot(file))
43	      .catch((err) => {
44	        log.error("failed to write heap snapshot", {
45	          error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
46	          file,
47	        })
48	      })
49	
50	    lock = false
51	  }
52	
53	  timer = setInterval(() => {
54	    void run()
55	  }, MINUTE)
56	  timer.unref?.()
57	}
58	
59	export * as Heap from "./heap"
```
